	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" >Roberto Firmino</h1>
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>

</p>
<div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Brazilian association football player</div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This name uses <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_name" title="Portuguese name">Portuguese naming customs</a>: the first or maternal <a href="/wiki/Surname" title="Surname">family name</a> is <i>Barbosa</i>&#32;and the second or paternal family name is <i>de Oliveira</i>.</div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p>

<p><b>Roberto Firmino Barbosa de Oliveira</b> (born 2 October 1991) is a Brazilian professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a> or <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">attacking midfielder</a> for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil national team</a>.
</p><p>After starting his career with <a href="/wiki/Figueirense_FC" title="Figueirense FC">Figueirense</a> in 2009, he spent four-and-a-half seasons at <a href="/wiki/TSG_1899_Hoffenheim" title="TSG 1899 Hoffenheim">Hoffenheim</a>. His 16 goals in 33 games for the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Bundesliga" title="201314 Bundesliga">201314 Bundesliga</a> season earned him the award for the league's Breakthrough Player. In July 2015, he signed for Premier League club <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a>. His creativity, goalscoring and work rate have earned him plaudits at Liverpool, with manager <a href="/wiki/J%C3%BCrgen_Klopp" title="Jürgen Klopp">Jürgen Klopp</a> referring to Firmino as the "engine" that propels the club's counter-attacking system.<sup id="cite_ref-engine_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-engine-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Liverpool_F.C._season" title="201819 Liverpool F.C. season">201819 season</a> he won the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2019 UEFA Champions League Final">UEFA Champions League</a>, and the following season won the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2019 UEFA Super Cup">UEFA Super Cup</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2019_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2019 FIFA Club World Cup">FIFA Club World Cup</a> after scoring the winner in the <a href="/wiki/2019_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_Final" title="2019 FIFA Club World Cup Final">final</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Premier_League" title="201920 Premier League">201920 Premier League</a> title, Liverpool's first league title in 30 years.
</p><p>Firmino made his international debut for <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> in November 2014. He represented the nation at the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2015 Copa América">2015 Copa América</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> and was part of the Brazil team that won the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 Copa América</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span></h3>
<p>Born in <a href="/wiki/Macei%C3%B3" title="Maceió">Maceió</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alagoas" title="Alagoas">Alagoas</a>, Firmino joined <a href="/wiki/Figueirense_FC" title="Figueirense FC">Figueirense</a>'s youth setup in 2008, aged 17, after starting out at <a href="/wiki/Clube_de_Regatas_Brasil" title="Clube de Regatas Brasil">CRB</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> He was discovered by a dentist, Marcellus Portella.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> With the latter, he was mainly used as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Defensive_midfielder" title="Midfielder">defensive midfielder</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Firmino made his professional debut on 24 October 2009, coming on as a half-time <a href="/wiki/Substitute_(association_football)" title="Substitute (association football)">substitute</a> for Toninho in a 12 home loss against <a href="/wiki/Associa%C3%A7%C3%A3o_Atl%C3%A9tica_Ponte_Preta" title="Associação Atlética Ponte Preta">Ponte Preta</a>, for the <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_B" title="Campeonato Brasileiro Série B">Série B</a> championship.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> In January 2010 he was promoted to the main squad.
</p><p>Firmino scored his first professional goal on 8 May 2010, netting the winner in an away success against <a href="/wiki/Associa%C3%A7%C3%A3o_Desportiva_S%C3%A3o_Caetano" title="Associação Desportiva São Caetano">São Caetano</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He contributed with eight goals in 36 appearances during <a href="/wiki/2010_Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_B" title="2010 Campeonato Brasileiro Série B">the season</a>, as <i>Figueira</i> returned to <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_A" title="Campeonato Brasileiro Série A">Série A</a> after a two-year absence.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hoffenheim">Hoffenheim</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Roberto_Firmino_2014_03_08.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Roberto_Firmino_2014_03_08.jpg/170px-Roberto_Firmino_2014_03_08.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="239" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Roberto_Firmino_2014_03_08.jpg/255px-Roberto_Firmino_2014_03_08.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Roberto_Firmino_2014_03_08.jpg/340px-Roberto_Firmino_2014_03_08.jpg 2x" data-file-width="344" data-file-height="483" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Roberto_Firmino_2014_03_08.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Firmino playing for <a href="/wiki/TSG_1899_Hoffenheim" title="TSG 1899 Hoffenheim">1899 Hoffenheim</a> in 2014</div></div></div>
<p>Firmino signed with <a href="/wiki/TSG_1899_Hoffenheim" title="TSG 1899 Hoffenheim">Hoffenheim</a> in December 2010, with the contract running until June 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He formally arrived at Hoffenheim on 1 January 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Then Hoffenheim manager Ernst Tanner commented that they were "pleased to hire a Brazilian talent".<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut a month later in a <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> defeat against <a href="/wiki/FSV_Mainz_05" class="mw-redirect" title="FSV Mainz 05">Mainz</a>, where he came on as a 75th-minute substitute for <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Rudy" title="Sebastian Rudy">Sebastian Rudy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-SW_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first goal for the club on 16 April, the only goal of a league victory against <a href="/wiki/Eintracht_Frankfurt" title="Eintracht Frankfurt">Eintracht Frankfurt</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was dropped from the first-team squad along with <a href="/wiki/Chinedu_Obasi" title="Chinedu Obasi">Chinedu Obasi</a> at the end of November 2011 for showing up late for training, missing the league match against <a href="/wiki/Bayer_Leverkusen" class="mw-redirect" title="Bayer Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> He scored two more goals that season, against Wolfsburg and <a href="/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mönchengladbach">Borussia Mönchengladbach</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-SW_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> In the 201213 season, Firmino made 36 appearances and scored seven goals.<sup id="cite_ref-SW_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In July 2013, Russian club <a href="/wiki/Lokomotiv_Moscow" class="mw-redirect" title="Lokomotiv Moscow">Lokomotiv Moscow</a> made a 12 million bid for Firmino.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Hoffenheim captain <a href="/wiki/Andreas_Beck_(footballer)" title="Andreas Beck (footballer)">Andreas Beck</a> hailed Firmino's development as "outstanding" in August 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> On 27 March 2014, Firmino extended his contract with the club, signing a three-year extension.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He finished the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Bundesliga" title="201314 Bundesliga">201314 Bundesliga</a> season tied as the fourth highest scorer with 16 goals,<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> and was named the league's Breakthrough Player.<sup id="cite_ref-break_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-break-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Liverpool">Liverpool</span></h3>
<p>On 23 June 2015, while he was competing for Brazil at the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2015 Copa América">Copa América</a>, Hoffenheim and Firmino agreed terms for him to transfer to <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> for up to £29 million on conclusion of the tournament, subject to a work permit.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Liverpool confirmed the signing the following day, subject to a medical.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> The deal was finalised on 4 July.<sup id="cite_ref-echo_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-echo-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201516_season">201516 season</span></h4>
<p>Firmino made his Liverpool debut in a pre-season friendly away to <a href="/wiki/Swindon_Town" class="mw-redirect" title="Swindon Town">Swindon Town</a> on 2 August,<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> and his league debut a week later, replacing <a href="/wiki/Jordon_Ibe" title="Jordon Ibe">Jordon Ibe</a> for the final 12 minutes of a 10 win at <a href="/wiki/Stoke_City" class="mw-redirect" title="Stoke City">Stoke City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> On 21 November, Firmino scored his first goal for Liverpool in a 41 victory over <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> at the <a href="/wiki/City_of_Manchester_Stadium" title="City of Manchester Stadium">City of Manchester Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> In January 2016, Firmino was described by Paul Little of the <i><a href="/wiki/Irish_Examiner" title="Irish Examiner">Irish Examiner</a></i> as steadily improving during his first season in England,<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> although an inability to combine with centre forward <a href="/wiki/Christian_Benteke" title="Christian Benteke">Christian Benteke</a> drew criticism.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, in 2016, Firmino's form improved as manager <a href="/wiki/J%C3%BCrgen_Klopp" title="Jürgen Klopp">Jürgen Klopp</a> played him alone up front in a <a href="/wiki/False_9" class="mw-redirect" title="False 9">false 9</a> role.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>  He scored braces against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> and <a href="/wiki/Norwich_City" class="mw-redirect" title="Norwich City">Norwich City</a> that month; the latter performance, in which he also assisted in a 54 win, earned comparisons to <a href="/wiki/Raheem_Sterling" title="Raheem Sterling">Raheem Sterling</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> With his form improved, Firmino was voted to be <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Liverpool_F.C._season#Liverpool_Standard_Chartered_Player_of_the_Month_award" title="201516 Liverpool F.C. season">Liverpool's Player of the Month in January</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Firmino ended the season as Liverpool's league top scorer with ten goals.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Roberto_Firmino_2017.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Roberto_Firmino_2017.jpg/170px-Roberto_Firmino_2017.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="343" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Roberto_Firmino_2017.jpg/255px-Roberto_Firmino_2017.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Roberto_Firmino_2017.jpg/340px-Roberto_Firmino_2017.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1202" data-file-height="2423" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Roberto_Firmino_2017.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Firmino playing for Liverpool in a Premier League game against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a>, 31 January 2017</div></div></div>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201617_season">201617 season</span></h4>
<p>On 23 August, Firmino scored his first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Liverpool_F.C._season" title="201617 Liverpool F.C. season">201617 season</a>, scoring in a 50 win over <a href="/wiki/Burton_Albion_F.C." title="Burton Albion F.C.">Burton Albion</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_EFL_Cup#Second_round" title="201617 EFL Cup">second round of the EFL Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Firmino scored his first league goals of the season in a 41 win over <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a>, scoring a brace, on 10 September.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> On 29 October, Firmino scored in a 42 win over <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a>, and on 6 November he scored in a 61 over <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a>; the latter result saw Liverpool move to 1st position in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Premier_League#League_table" title="201617 Premier League">league table</a>, the first time under <a href="/wiki/J%C3%BCrgen_Klopp" title="Jürgen Klopp">Klopp</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> On 27 December, he scored in a 41 win over <a href="/wiki/Stoke_City_F.C." title="Stoke City F.C.">Stoke City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> On 21 January 2017, Firmino scored a brace in a 23 home defeat to <a href="/wiki/Swansea_City_A.F.C." title="Swansea City A.F.C.">Swansea City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> On 4 March, he scored the opening goal in a 31 win over <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> On 8 April, Firmino scored the winning goal in a 21 win over <a href="/wiki/Stoke_City_F.C." title="Stoke City F.C.">Stoke City</a>, and also scored the winning goal in the game against <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C." title="West Bromwich Albion F.C.">West Bromwich Albion</a>, which Liverpool won 10, on 16 April.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Firmino finished the season with 12 goals in 38 appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201718_season">201718 season</span></h4>
<p>Before the start of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Liverpool_F.C._season" title="201718 Liverpool F.C. season">201718 season</a>, Firmino switched his shirt number to 9, with new signing <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Salah" title="Mohamed Salah">Mohamed Salah</a> taking his number 11.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Firmino scored his first goal of the new season on 12 August, scoring a penalty in a 33 draw with <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> On 17 December, he scored in a 40 away win over <a href="/wiki/AFC_Bournemouth" title="AFC Bournemouth">AFC Bournemouth</a>; a result which saw Liverpool become the first team in <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> history to win four consecutive away games by a margin of at least three goals.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:151px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Spartak_Moscow-_Liverpool_Firmino.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3c/Spartak_Moscow-_Liverpool_Firmino.jpg" decoding="async" width="149" height="210" class="thumbimage" data-file-width="149" data-file-height="210" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Spartak_Moscow-_Liverpool_Firmino.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Firmino with Liverpool during a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> match against Spartak Moscow in 2017</div></div></div>
<p>On 5 January 2018, during a <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_FA_Cup" title="201718 FA Cup">FA Cup</a> match against rivals <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Firmino was the subject of controversy following a clash with Everton defender <a href="/wiki/Mason_Holgate" title="Mason Holgate">Mason Holgate</a>. Holgate pushed Firmino into the advertising boards, which was followed by the pair exchanging words, with Firmino seemingly insulting the player. Following the match, Holgate accused Firmino of racially abusing him, which he denied. A day later, the <a href="/wiki/The_Football_Association" title="The Football Association">Football Association</a> opened an investigation on the matter.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Nearly two months later, after they had took statements from 12 different players, several referees and consulted two <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_language" title="Portuguese language">Portuguese</a> <a href="/wiki/Lip_reading" title="Lip reading">lip-readers</a>, the Football Association cleared Firmino of any offence as a result of "insufficient evidence".<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 14 January, Firmino scored in a 43 home win over <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a>; which saw Liverpool end City's unbeaten league run.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> On 10 April, he scored in a 21 win over <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Manchester_City_v_Liverpool" title="201718 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">second leg of the quarter-finals of the Champions League</a>; which saw Liverpool advance to the semi-finals with a 51 aggregate win.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Firmino started and played the whole 90 minutes in the <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2018 UEFA Champions League Final">2018 UEFA Champions League Final</a>, with Liverpool losing 31.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the season, Firmino, <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Salah" title="Mohamed Salah">Mohamed Salah</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philippe_Coutinho" title="Philippe Coutinho">Philippe Coutinho</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sadio_Man%C3%A9" title="Sadio Mané">Sadio Mané</a> made up a prolific attacking quarter, dubbed the "Fab Four", in reference to the rock band <a href="/wiki/The_Beatles" title="The Beatles">The Beatles</a>, also from the same city as the club.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Following the mid-season exit of <a href="/wiki/Philippe_Coutinho" title="Philippe Coutinho">Coutinho</a>, the three remaining players were dubbed as the "Fab Three", with the trio having a total of 91 goals between them at the end of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Firmino was Liverpool's joint top goalscorer in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201718 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>, together with <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Salah" title="Mohamed Salah">Salah</a>, with 11 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Firmino was also included in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League#Squad_of_the_Season" title="201718 UEFA Champions League">201718 UEFA Champions League Squad of the Season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Liverpool_F.C._season" title="201718 Liverpool F.C. season">201718 season</a> was Firmino's most prolific in his <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> career; as he scored 27 goals in all competitions.<sup id="cite_ref-Liverpool_FC_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Liverpool_FC-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201819_season">201819 season</span></h4>
<p>After going goalless in all three matches played in August, Firmino scored his first goal of the season in a 21 Premier League win over <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a> on 1 September.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> On 15 September he scored in Liverpool's 21 league win over <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur" class="mw-redirect" title="Tottenham Hotspur">Spurs</a> at Wembley, a game that saw him leave the field 15 minutes before the end with an eye injury.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Three days later he came off the bench to score the stoppage time winner in Liverpool's 32 Champions League win against <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> at Anfield.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> On 29 December, Firmino scored his first Liverpool <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> in a 51 win over <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>, scoring two goals in three minutes and a second half penalty.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> On 19 January 2019, he scored Liverpool's 1000th goal at <a href="/wiki/Anfield" title="Anfield">Anfield</a> in the Premier League era when he netted in a 43 win over <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 1 June, Firmino started for Liverpool in the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2019 UEFA Champions League Final">2019 UEFA Champions League Final</a> against Tottenham, making a comeback after missing the last few weeks of the season with injury. Firmino lasted 60 minutes before being substituted as Liverpool won the match 20 to claim the title.<sup id="cite_ref-McNulty_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McNulty-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201920_season">201920 season</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Liverpool_vs._Chelsea,_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_17.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_17.jpg/220px-Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_17.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_17.jpg/330px-Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_17.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_17.jpg/440px-Liverpool_vs._Chelsea%2C_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_17.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1050" data-file-height="700" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Liverpool_vs._Chelsea,_UEFA_Super_Cup_2019-08-14_17.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Firmino during the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2019 UEFA Super Cup">2019 UEFA Super Cup</a> final against Chelsea</div></div></div>
<p>On 14 August 2019, Firmino came off the bench in the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2019 UEFA Super Cup">2019 UEFA Super Cup</a> final against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> in a match that Liverpool won 54 on penalties. The game had finished 22 after 120 minutes, with Firmino setting up both goals for <a href="/wiki/Sadio_Man%C3%A9" title="Sadio Mané">Sadio Mané</a>, before Firmino scored the first penalty in the shoot-out win.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> On 31 August 2019, Firmino became the first Brazilian player to score 50 goals in the Premier League when he netted the third and final goal in a 30 win over <a href="/wiki/Burnley_F.C." title="Burnley F.C.">Burnley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>At the <a href="/wiki/2019_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2019 FIFA Club World Cup">2019 FIFA Club World Cup</a> in December, Firmino scored the winning goal in a 21 semi-final win over <a href="/wiki/C.F._Monterrey" title="C.F. Monterrey">Monterrey</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> Three days later he was named man of the match in the <a href="/wiki/2019_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_Final" title="2019 FIFA Club World Cup Final">final</a> after scoring the winner against <a href="/wiki/Clube_de_Regatas_do_Flamengo" title="Clube de Regatas do Flamengo">Flamengo</a> as Liverpool won the competition for the first time.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:20180610_FIFA_Friendly_Match_Austria_vs._Brazil_Hierl%C3%A4nder_Firmino_850_0108.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/20180610_FIFA_Friendly_Match_Austria_vs._Brazil_Hierl%C3%A4nder_Firmino_850_0108.jpg/220px-20180610_FIFA_Friendly_Match_Austria_vs._Brazil_Hierl%C3%A4nder_Firmino_850_0108.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/20180610_FIFA_Friendly_Match_Austria_vs._Brazil_Hierl%C3%A4nder_Firmino_850_0108.jpg/330px-20180610_FIFA_Friendly_Match_Austria_vs._Brazil_Hierl%C3%A4nder_Firmino_850_0108.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/20180610_FIFA_Friendly_Match_Austria_vs._Brazil_Hierl%C3%A4nder_Firmino_850_0108.jpg/440px-20180610_FIFA_Friendly_Match_Austria_vs._Brazil_Hierl%C3%A4nder_Firmino_850_0108.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4901" data-file-height="3267" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:20180610_FIFA_Friendly_Match_Austria_vs._Brazil_Hierl%C3%A4nder_Firmino_850_0108.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Firmino playing against <a href="/wiki/Austria_national_football_team" title="Austria national football team">Austria</a> in 2018</div></div></div>
<p>Firmino said that it was his "dream" to play in the national team though he had no "contact with national team manager <a href="/wiki/Dunga" title="Dunga">Dunga</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> On 23 October 2014, Firmino received his first call up to <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil national football team</a> for the friendly matches against <a href="/wiki/Turkey_national_football_team" title="Turkey national football team">Turkey</a> and <a href="/wiki/Austria_national_football_team" title="Austria national football team">Austria</a>. He commented, "I'm very happy about the nomination and would especially like to thank the team".<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> He debuted in a 40 win over Turkey on 12 November, replacing fellow debutant <a href="/wiki/Luiz_Adriano" title="Luiz Adriano">Luiz Adriano</a> for the last 17 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> Firmino scored his first goal  six days later in the latter match, a 21 away win.<sup id="cite_ref-goal_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goal-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2015, Firmino was included in Brazil's 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2015 Copa América">2015 Copa América</a> to be held in Chile.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> On 21 June, he scored in a 21 defeat of <a href="/wiki/Venezuela_national_football_team" title="Venezuela national football team">Venezuela</a> to qualify the <i>Seleção</i> for the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_knockout_stage" title="2015 Copa América knockout stage">knockout stage</a> as <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Group_C" title="2015 Copa América Group C">Group C</a> winners.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2018 he was named in Tite's final <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">23 man squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_World_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="2018 World Cup">2018 World Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> On 2 July, Firmino scored Brazil's second goal in a 20 win over Mexico in the round of sixteen having come on as a late substitute.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2019, Firmino was included in Brazil's 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 Copa América</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> Firmino played all 90 minutes of the final as Brazil won 31 to lift their ninth Copa América title.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Russia-Brazil_2018_(11)_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Russia-Brazil_2018_%2811%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Russia-Brazil_2018_%2811%29_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="314" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Russia-Brazil_2018_%2811%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Russia-Brazil_2018_%2811%29_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Russia-Brazil_2018_%2811%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Russia-Brazil_2018_%2811%29_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="487" data-file-height="900" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Russia-Brazil_2018_(11)_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Firmino is known for his creativity, link-up play, goalscoring and workrate.</div></div></div>
<p>At Hoffenheim, Firmino primarily played as an <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">attacking midfielder</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> or as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Second_striker" title="Forward (association football)">second striker</a>, but was also used as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a>, <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">winger</a> or <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central midfielder</a>, with Firmino using his speed, close control and vision wherever he is deployed.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> After initially starting as a left winger at Liverpool under <a href="/wiki/Brendan_Rodgers" title="Brendan Rodgers">Brendan Rodgers</a>, new manager <a href="/wiki/J%C3%BCrgen_Klopp" title="Jürgen Klopp">Jürgen Klopp</a> used Firmino more centrally, initially as a <a href="/wiki/False_9" class="mw-redirect" title="False 9">False 9</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> However, after impressing under Klopp's pressing system, Firmino established himself as Liverpool's first choice <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Centre-forward" title="Forward (association football)">centre-forward</a> by the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Liverpool_F.C._season" title="201718 Liverpool F.C. season">201718 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> Ian Doyle of the <i>Liverpool Echo</i> referred to him as "a true Liverpool number nine", whose "numbers are up there with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Kane" title="Harry Kane">Harry Kane</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Sergio Agüero</a>."<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Ryan_Babel" title="Ryan Babel">Ryan Babel</a>, a teammate of Firmino's at Hoffenheim, described him as "A tricky player. He can dribble, shoot, he has a great shot, he can play a lot of through balls and his assists are very good", while also praising a heading ability which would not be common amongst other players of Firmino's slender build and relatively small stature,<sup id="cite_ref-echo_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-echo-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> a unique trait which journalist and <a href="/wiki/ESPN" title="ESPN">ESPN</a> contributor <a href="/wiki/Michael_Cox_(journalist)" title="Michael Cox (journalist)">Michael Cox</a> has also noted.<sup id="cite_ref-simple_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-simple-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Babel also stated that Firmino had a humble mentality and no problems with attitude.<sup id="cite_ref-echo_23-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-echo-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Manager <a href="/wiki/Hemerson_Maria" title="Hemerson Maria">Hemerson Maria</a> also stated that he was impressed with Firmino's "strong personality and mentality."<sup id="cite_ref-shy,_strong-willed_94-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shy,_strong-willed-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> In addition to his technical skills, creativity, link-up play, and goalscoring, Firmino has also been praised by his managers, teammates, and pundits for his positional sense, mobility, intelligent movement, and ability to make attacking runs off the ball, which often draws opposing players out of position and creates space for his teammates.<sup id="cite_ref-simple_93-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-simple-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Firmino-key-Liverpool_95-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Firmino-key-Liverpool-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-man_who_discovered_Firmino_96-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-man_who_discovered_Firmino-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to his energy and defensive work-rate off the ball,<sup id="cite_ref-Firmino-key-Liverpool_95-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Firmino-key-Liverpool-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-man_who_discovered_Firmino_96-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-man_who_discovered_Firmino-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> Klopp has referred to Firmino as the "engine" that propels the team's relentless counter-attacking system; "If he loses the ball, he fights for it back. If he loses it again, he fights for it. He looks like the engine of the team."<sup id="cite_ref-engine_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-engine-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> The suitability of Firmino's playing style to Klopp's pressing system has meant that Firmino was referred to as "Liverpool's most important player" on several occasions during the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Liverpool_F.C._season" title="201617 Liverpool F.C. season">201617</a> and <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Liverpool_F.C._season" title="201718 Liverpool F.C. season">201718</a> seasons.<sup id="cite_ref-Firmino-key-Liverpool_95-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Firmino-key-Liverpool-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> Due to Firmino's wide range of skills, <a href="/wiki/Thierry_Henry" title="Thierry Henry">Thierry Henry</a> described him as the most complete <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Striker" title="Forward (association football)">striker</a> in the [Premier] League."<sup id="cite_ref-shy,_strong-willed_94-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shy,_strong-willed-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Firmino is also well known for his popular "no-look" goals.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> One of his best known <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">goal celebrations</a>, 'the Matador', features in the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_(video_game_series)" title="FIFA (video game series)"><i>FIFA</i></a> video game <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_19" title="FIFA 19">FIFA 19</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span></h2>
<p>Firmino married Larissa Pereira in his hometown in June 2017. They have two daughters.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> Firmino has been given the affectionate nickname "Bobby" by Liverpool fans and players  a <a href="/wiki/Hypocorism" title="Hypocorism">shortening</a> of his first name "Roberto".<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In December 2016, Firmino was arrested for drink driving. He was fined £20,000 and had his driving licence revoked for a year when sentenced at <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_Magistrates%27_Court" title="Liverpool Magistrates&#39; Court">Liverpool Magistrates' Court</a> in February 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-banned_105-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-banned-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In addition to his native <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_language" title="Portuguese language">Portuguese</a>, Firmino also speaks <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a> and <a href="/wiki/German_language" title="German language">German</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
